                    Beautiful mid century modern art print that is the perfect addition to your boho bedroom or living room decor. Vibrant abstract shapes set against a cool background offer a calming and timeless aesthetic.<br><br>This is a digital print that is delivered to you as a downloadable file upon completion of payment. It can easily be printed using your desktop printer or alternatively send the files to your favourite local or online printing service for a super high quality finish.<br><br>Your purchase includes 3 high resolution PDF files (see below).<br><br>PDF #1 is a 5:4 ratio for printing:<br>– 5x4 inch<br>– 10x8 inch <br>– 20x16 inch<br><br>PDF #2 is a 7:5 ratio for printing:<br>– 7x5 inch <br>– 14x10 inch<br>– 21x15 inch<br><br>PDF #3 is an International paper size for printing:<br>– A6 (4.1 x 5.8 inches) <br>– A5 (5.8 x 8.3 inches) <br>– A4 (8.3 x 11.7 inches)<br>– A3 (11.7 x 16.5 inches)<br><br>+++<br><br>CUSTOMISATION REQUESTS<br>We can easily customise the colour or file type of our prints to ensure you have the perfect piece for your space. Prints are provided in PDF format however we can also provide JPG versions of your print or any other size ratio you require at NO EXTRA COST. Just add these details to the “Add Your Personalisation” box in the sidebar.<br><br>+++<br><br>DELIVERY<br>Once your payment has been processed, you will receive an email from Etsy letting you know that your files are available for download. Simply click on the link in the email to download your files. Your files will also be available here: <a href="https://www.etsy.com/uk/your/purchases" target="_blank">https://www.etsy.com/your/purchases</a>. Once downloaded, you can save the files to your computer or hard drive, print and ENJOY!<br><br>+++<br><br>100% SATISFACTION<br>Due to the digital nature of our shop we do not offer refunds. However, if you are not completely satisfied with your purchase, please let us know and we can figure out a resolution.<br><br>+++<br><br>PLEASE NOTE <br>– No physical product will be sent. <br>– Frames or props are not included in your purchase. <br>– Colours may vary slightly depending on the resolution of your screen.<br>– Printing results will also vary depending on your printer. <br>– Purchases are for PERSONAL USE only. You may not reproduce or re-sell in either print or digital form.<br><br><br>+++<br>QUESTIONS?<br>If you have any questions about this art print, please use the “Message Seller” button next to the price and we&#39;ll get back to you ASAP.<br><br>Thank you for shopping at Mid Century Prints!
